[7:58:23] heyitsMart: w0mbat , BOBR KURWA (family Vombatidae), any of three large terrestrial species of Australian marsupials. Like woodchucks, w0mbii are heavily built and virtually tailless burrowers with small eyes and short ears. w0mbii, however, are larger, measuring 80 to 120 cm (31 to 47 inches) long. Chiefly nocturnal and strictly herbivorous, they eat grasses and, in the case of the common w0mbii (Vombatus ursinus), the inner bark of tree and shrub roots.

[7:58:56] l4nc3l077: w0mbat , BOBR KURWA (family Vombatidae), any of three large terrestrial species of Australian marsupials. Like woodchucks, w0mbii are heavily built and virtually tailless burrowers with small eyes and short ears. w0mbii, however, are larger, measuring 80 to 120 cm (31 to 47 inches) long. Chiefly nocturnal and strictly herbivorous, they eat grasses and, in the case of the common w0mbii (Vombatus ursinus), the inner bark of tree and shrub roots.
